The hotel's response to this matter The handling is not sincere and the management of the hotel is very regrettable.

Hotel closest to Beijing Botanical Garden.
You can get there in 1 station by subway!
It was an old hotel, but the material was rather luxurious, so it was very impressive to have an antique interior.
I couldn't take a picture of breakfast, but the breakfast menu was also diverse!
Most of the staff were friendly, especially the 'wumeibo' staff was really nice.You even remember the name because you left an impression!
I'm taking good memories with me.I'll be back next time!
